country_event = { #Death of King George V
	id = nfa.4
	title = nfa.4.t
	desc = nfa.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_death_george

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by the CAN event

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.4 option nfa.4.a"
		name = nfa.4.a #The King is dead, long live the king
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.5 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Lion in Canada
	id = nfa.5
	title = nfa.5.t
	desc = nfa.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_edward2

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.5 option nfa.5.a"
		name = nfa.5.a #Time to return home
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = committed_to_return_home
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = committed_to_return_home
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.6 days = 14 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Book Competition - Setup
	id = nfa.6
	title = nfa.6.t
	desc = nfa.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_books

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.6 option nfa.6.a"
		name = nfa.6.a #Let's see what they wrote
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.7 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { #Set up the variables for the power struggle
			set_variable = {
				var = Pet_influence
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Mor_influence
				value = 2
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Pet_corruption
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Competition_Loop_Counter
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Book Competition - Books
	id = nfa.7
	title = nfa.7.t
	desc = nfa.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_books

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.7 option nfa.7.a"
		name = nfa.7.a #Support Mordacq
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.8 days = 10 }
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.7 option nfa.7.b"
		name = nfa.7.b #Support CdG
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.9 days = 10 }
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.7 option nfa.7.c"
		name = nfa.7.c #Let it run it's course

			base = 20

				factor = 0

					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}

			}
			clamp_variable = {

				min = 0
				max = 30
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Franchet d'Espèrey Retires
	id = nfa.13
	title = nfa.13.t
	desc = nfa.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_TheOtherMarshal

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.13 option nfa.13.a"
		name = nfa.13.a #Pass the Torch to the Bear
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		retire_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey
		NFA_henri_mordacq = { promote_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.16 days = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.13 option nfa.13.b"
		name = nfa.13.b #Lion Undivided
		ai_chance = {
			base = 32
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0 }
			set_country_flag = Petain_headstart_cf #Gives Petain a slight boost in the Fight for Influence
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		retire_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.19 days = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.13 option nfa.13.c"
		name = nfa.13.c #Young Guard
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		retire_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey
		NFA_charles_de_gaulle = { promote_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.43 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #New Union Sacree
	id = nfa.96
	immediate = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;NFA DEMOCRACY;[GetDateText]"
	}
	title = nfa.96.t
	desc = nfa.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_NFA_Assembly

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.96 option nfa.96.a"
		name = nfa.96.a #Vive La Republique!
		add_political_power = 25
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_union_sacree_coalition_tooltip
		activate_advisor = NFA_francois_de_la_rocque_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NFA.coalition_stability = 0.25 }
			country_event = { id = nfa.97 days = 14 }
			country_event = { id = nfa.270 days = 40 random_days = 50 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_lar = yes }
				create_operative_leader = {
					name = "George Groussard"
					GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_george_groussard_operative
					traits = {
						operative_commando
					}
					bypass_recruitment = yes
					nationalities = { NFA FRA }
				}
			}
			NFA_henri_mordacq = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
					promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = NFA_henri_mordacq_dem_leader_desc
							ideology = social_conservative_subtype
							traits = { NFA_Bear_Elect }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = NATFRA_Democracy_Restored
			random_other_country = { news_event = worldnews.444 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen }
				clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
				NFA_remove_de_gaulle_military_ideas = yes
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen }
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
}

					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 1
				}

					var = Pet_corruption

					max = 30

				add_stability = 0.01

		}

				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 1
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					min = 0
					max = 30
				}
			}
			else = {
				army_experience = 0.05
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.27 option nfa.27.b"
		name = nfa.27.b #Crack down on incoming Mail
		trigger = {
			has_political_power > 0
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		add_political_power = -5
		add_war_support = -0.025
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Mail_crack_down
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Competition Counter
	id = nfa.28
	title = nfa.28.t
	desc = nfa.28.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.28 option nfa.28.a"
		name = nfa.28.a
		if = { #Loop Again
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Competition_Loop_Counter
					value = 1
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = Mordacq_Airwaves
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NATFRA_CSN
					has_country_flag = NATFRA_Democracy_Restored
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
						has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
				NFA_remove_de_gaulle_military_ideas = yes
				clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			#Do nothing to end the loop
		}
		else = { #Someone is a Winner
			clr_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			if = { #Check if Mordacq has more influence than Petain
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = Mor_influence
						value = Pet_influence
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = nfa.35 days = 7 } # Mordacq coups Petain
				set_country_flag = NFA_Napoleon_0
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = nfa.39 days = 15 } # Petain has more influence
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Corruption Check
	id = nfa.30
	title = nfa.30.t
	desc = nfa.30.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.30 option nfa.30.a"
		name = nfa.30.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 6
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.32 days = 1 } # Corruption still coming
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NFA_event_31
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 5
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 3
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.31 days = 1 } # High Corruption warning
			country_event = { id = nfa.30 days = 7 } #Loop the checker
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
				has_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.30 days = 7 } #Loop the checker
		}
		else = {
			# Nothing to end this loop
		}
	}
}

			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
				}
				clr_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			}
		}
	}
}

				active = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_1_nobel
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA except Brittany
			GER_transfer_NFA_except_Brittany = yes
			# Make Brittany
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
			# Border Fort Dismantlement
			NFA_Border_Dismantlement = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
			# Military Disarmament
			NFA_Military_Accords_Harsh = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = NFA
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
			set_global_flag = ENT_france_agree_mittel
			NFA = {
				CAN_remove_from_iedc = yes
				set_country_flag = CAN_refused_iedc
				GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_1
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA except Greater Belgium and Brittany
			GER_transfer_NFA_except_Belgium_and_Brittany = yes
			# Expanded Calais
			NFA_Greater_Belgium_to_GER = yes
			# Make Brittany
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
			# Border Fort Dismantlement
			NFA_Border_Dismantlement = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
			# Military Disarmament
			NFA_Military_Accords_Harsh = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = NFA
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
			set_global_flag = ENT_france_agree_mittel
			NFA = {
				CAN_remove_from_iedc = yes
				set_country_flag = CAN_refused_iedc
				GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = nfa.157.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_map_france

	trigger = {
		any_owned_state = { region = 19 }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.157 option nfa.157.a"
		name = nfa.157.a #France should be made whole
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 19
			}
			transfer_state_to = NFA
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.157 option nfa.157.b"
		name = nfa.157.b #Keep Dunkirk, share the rest
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				region = 19
				NOT = { state = 29 } #Don't give away Dunkirk
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 19
				NOT = { state = 29 } #Don't give away Dunkirk
			}
			transfer_state_to = NFA
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.157 option nfa.157.c"
		name = nfa.157.c #We will keep the territory
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -100
	}

country_event = { #Returning state events success
	id = nfa.193
	title = nfa.193.t
	desc = nfa.193.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.193 option nfa.193.a"
		name = nfa.193.a #Excellent!
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GBR }
			event_target:return_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { CAN = { PREV = { is_core_of = PREV } } } #syntax is needed to prevent tag alias shenanigans
						NOT = { is_core_of = AST }
						NOT = { is_core_of = NZL }
						NOT = { is_core_of = SAF }
						NOT = { is_core_of = RAJ }
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_state_claim = event_target:return_state
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #New Elections
	id = nfa.222

		trigger = { has_country_flag = NATFRA_Concentration_Holds_On_cf }

		trigger = { has_country_flag = NATFRA_CSN }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SWE_Elections

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.222 option nfa.222.a"
		name = nfa.222.a #The Radicals win a majority
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = NATFRA_Concentration_Holds_On_cf
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_election option = NFA_ELECTION_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		NFA_henri_mordacq = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
				promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = NFA_henri_mordacq_dem_leader_desc
						ideology = social_liberal_subtype
						traits = { NFA_Old_Bear }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea_with_trait = KR_parliament_sic } }
			activate_advisor = NFA_national_assembly_sic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_country_flag = NATFRA_Radical_Win_cf
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.222 option nfa.222.b"
		name = nfa.222.b #The Bloc National comes out on top
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = NATFRA_Concentration_Holds_On_cf
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_election option = NFA_ELECTION_SOCLIB }
			}
		}
		NFA_henri_mordacq = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
				promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = NFA_henri_mordacq_dem_leader_desc
						ideology = social_conservative_subtype
						traits = { NFA_Old_Bear }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea_with_trait = KR_parliament_sic } }

			ideology = social_conservative

	id = nfa.223

	desc = nfa.223.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.223 option nfa.223.a"
		name = nfa.223.a #Some semblance of Democracy
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_election option = NFA_ELECTION_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea_with_trait = KR_parliament_sic } }
			activate_advisor = NFA_national_assembly_sic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_tt_PSF_becomes_ade
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value = party_popularity@social_conservative }
			set_temp_variable = { NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse = 0 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { var = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse value = party_popularity@social_conservative }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse }
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value }
			NFA_francois_de_la_rocque = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = NFA_francois_de_la_rocque_leader_desc
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
							traits = { NFA_Colonel }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat elections_allowed = yes }
		}
		set_country_flag = NATFRA_semblance_of_democracy_cf
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.223 option nfa.223.b"
		name = nfa.223.b #Maintain military rule
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_election option = NFA_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		activate_advisor = NFA_georges_lamirand_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_tt_PSF_becomes_pau
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value = party_popularity@social_conservative }
			set_temp_variable = { NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse = 0 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { var = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse value = party_popularity@social_conservative }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse }
			add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value }
			NFA_francois_de_la_rocque = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }

		text = nfa.251.d.autonomy #Autonomy
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = NATFRA_Promote_Autonomy }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_AFFlavorAristocracy

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.251 option nfa.251.a"
		name = nfa.251.a #Let us continue our efforts to incorporate African peoples as French Citizens
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = NATFRA_Civ_Mission }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.075
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = NFA_native_unrest_3
			add_idea = NFA_unequal_citizenship
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_Algiers_Conference_Civ_effect
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.251 option nfa.251.b"
		name = nfa.251.b #Continue widesweeping autonomy across the country
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = NATFRA_Promote_Autonomy }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 75
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_Algiers_Conference_AF_effect
		remove_ideas = NFA_native_unrest_4
		hidden_effect = {
			# French Saharan Africa #
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance }
					NOT = {
						state = 834 #Gambia
						state = 700 #Sierra Leone
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance
				}
				clr_state_flag = nfa_state_colonial_resistance_flag
				clear_variable = NFA_colonial_resistance_target_var
				clear_variable = NFA_colonial_resistance_compliance_var

				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Autonomous_State }
				force_enable_resistance = { occupier = NFA clear = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_decision = Transahara_Phase_Two

			}

					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
			}
		}

country_event = { #Conclusion of the Purge chain
	id = nfa.317
	title = nfa.317.t
	desc = nfa.317.d
	picture = GFX_AF_trial_dec_1

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.317 option nfa.317.a"
		name = nfa.317.a #A new bonus
		remove_ideas = NFA_republican_remnants
		set_country_flag = NFA_AF_purge_decisions_over
		if = { #Give the idea of the most clicked option
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_low > NFA_AF_purged_high
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_low > NFA_AF_purged_medium
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_low_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_medium > NFA_AF_purged_low
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_medium > NFA_AF_purged_high
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_medium_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_high > NFA_AF_purged_low
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_high > NFA_AF_purged_medium
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_high_idea
		}
		# If there is a tie situation
		else = {
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_medium_idea
		}
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_low
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_medium
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_high
	}
}

	title = nfa.513.t
	desc = nfa.513.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_FlavorWomenVote

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.513 option nfa.513.a"
		name = nfa.513.a #Pour toutes!
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.514 days = 100 } #Down with Marianne
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Meeting with his Holiness - AF event
	id = nfa.517
	title = nfa.517.t
	desc = {
		text = nfa.517.d.angrypope
		trigger = {
			NOT = { PAP = { has_country_leader = { character = PAP_achille_liennart } } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.517.d.nicepope
		trigger = {
			PAP = { has_country_leader = { character = PAP_achille_liennart } }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_pope

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = PAP
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.517 option nfa.517.a"
		name = nfa.517.a #A joyous occasion
		add_stability = 0.02
		if = {
			limit = { PAP = { has_country_leader = { character = PAP_achille_liennart } } }
			add_political_power = 20
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PAP
			modifier = NFA_PAP_meeting
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = NFA
					modifier = NFA_PAP_meeting
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.535 days = 120 } #Pontifical Zouaves
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to check if post-war events can fire, depending on owned states and months
	id = nfa.529

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.529 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 762 #Nice
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.518 days = 8 random_days = 48 } #Restoration of Monaco
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 21 #Marseille
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.8.29
						date < 1939.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.8.29
						date < 1940.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.8.29
						date < 1941.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.8.29
						date < 1942.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.8.29
						date < 1943.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.8.29
						date < 1944.10.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.530 days = 2 } #Festival d'Avignon
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.179 days = 95 } #The question of Montmartre
			country_event = { id = nfa.531 days = 450 } #A mosque in Paris?
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.6.29
						date < 1939.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.6.29
						date < 1940.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.6.29
						date < 1941.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.6.29
						date < 1942.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.6.29
						date < 1943.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.6.29
						date < 1944.8.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.532 days = 2 } #First New Tour de France
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.1.29
						date < 1939.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.1.29
						date < 1940.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.1.29
						date < 1941.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.1.29
						date < 1942.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.1.29
						date < 1943.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.1.29
						date < 1944.2.25
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.540 days = 2 } #Emmaus
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 15 #Normandy
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.533 days = 160 } #Rouen Reconstruction
			country_event = { id = nfa.534 days = 250 } #Tank in Vimoutiers
		}
		country_event = { id = nfa.529 days = 45 } #Loop the event without jumping over months
	}
}

	id = nfa.539

	trigger = {

				has_war_with = EGY
				has_war_with = HEJ

				has_war_with = SAU
			}
		}

# French Guinea and Upper Volta

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - French Guinea
	id = nfa.443

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			806 = { #Guinea
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			808 = { #Upper Volta
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF }
	}

	option = { #Mission Attacked - 444
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.443 option 1"
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Guinea
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.34
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
		country_event = nfa.444
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 108 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Volta kings dispute - 471
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.443 option 2"
		trigger = {
			808 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
				808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Upper Volta
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.125
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
		country_event = nfa.471
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 108 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Infrastructure Sabotaged - 445
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.443 option 3"
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Upper Volta
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.445
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 144 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Garrison Attacked - 446
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.443 option 4"
		trigger = {
			808 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Upper Volta
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.446
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 216 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #no effect
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.443 option 5"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.16
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.83
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 108 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - Senegal
	id = nfa.467

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
			has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = nfa.467 days = 158 random_days = 36 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Miner strike - 468
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.467 option 1"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
		country_event = nfa.468
	}

	option = { #Resentment spreading to Lower classes - 469
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.467 option 2"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 22
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.14
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
		country_event = nfa.469
	}

	option = { #Evolués support the idea of independence - 470
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.467 option 3"

			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 12
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
		country_event = nfa.470
	}

	option = { #Nothing happens
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.467 option 4"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.08
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.42
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.54
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Colony Revolts (donotlog)
	id = nfa.601
	title = nfa.601.t
	desc = nfa.601.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOM_intro

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NFA_active_rebellion
			set_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_@event_target:revolter
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = NFA_crush_resistance target = event_target:revolter }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = event_target:revolter }
				transfer_state_to = event_target:revolter
			}
			event_target:revolter = {
				log = "KR_Event_Logging;[THIS.GetTag] REVOLTS AGAINST NFA;[GetDateText]"
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						load_oob = [OOB_NAME]
					}
					OOB_NAME = "[revolter.GetTag]_revolt"
				}
				every_controlled_state = {
					every_neighbor_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
							NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						}
						add_resistance = 8
						add_compliance = -4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.601.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = FRA } #Don't add the idea if during 2WK
				NOT = { NFA_has_multiple_african_revolts = yes } #Don't add the idea if NFA has lots of revolts
				NOT = { has_idea = NFA_small_native_revolt } #Don't add the idea twice
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_small_native_revolt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NFA_has_multiple_african_revolts = yes
				has_idea = NFA_small_native_revolt
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_revolts_getting_out_of_hand
			remove_ideas = NFA_small_native_revolt
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:revolter
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.601.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -75
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation }
				}
			}
			add_resistance = 12
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Collapse of the French Republic if killed or someone got algeria
	id = nfa.623
	title = nfa.623.t
	desc = nfa.623.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_AFFlavorMarianne

	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		OR = {
			has_capitulated = yes
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 460
				controls_state = 865
				controls_state = 459
				controls_state = 805
				controls_state = 458
			}
		}
		NOT = { #One Major French city is back in our hands
			16 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			19 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			20 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			21 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.623 option nfa.623.a"
		name = nfa.623.a
		### Morocco
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = MOR
				}
				country_exists = MOR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 290 #The Rif
						state = 699 #Rio de Oro
						state = 968 #Ifni
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = MOR
			}
		}

		### Kill off NFA
		force_capitulate = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENT = {
						is_ai = no
						has_war_with = EGY
					}
					EGY = {
						is_subject = no
						OR = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}
				}
				ENT = {
					country_event = { id = nfa.625 days = 1 } #Do you want to continue the war?
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ENT = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_war_with = EGY
					}
					EGY = {
						is_subject = no
						OR = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}
				}
				EGY = {
					country_event = { id = nfa.626 days = 2 } #ENT sues for peace
				}
			}
		}

		### Peace off the rebels
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				is_valid_peace_target = yes
				OR = {
					tag = TUN
					tag = CHA
					tag = NGR
					tag = MLI
					tag = MRT
					tag = VOL
					tag = GNA
					tag = IVO
					tag = SEN
					tag = SIE
				}
			}
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			ROOT = {
				clr_country_flag = NFA_active_rebellion
				clr_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_@PREV
			}
		}

		### Free all puppets
		every_subject_country = {
			overlord = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}

		### Kill Off NFA
		force_capitulate = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.626 option nfa.626.a"
		name = nfa.626.a #Accept the peace
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 50
		ENT = {
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			country_event = nfa.627 #EGY accepts peace
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.626 option nfa.626.b"
		name = nfa.626.b #Never shall there be peace!
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		ENT = {
			country_event = nfa.628 #EGY refuses peace
		}
	}
}

		name = nfa.629.a #Return to France
		trigger = {
			tag = BRI
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			NFA = { change_tag_from = ROOT }

				annex_country = {
					target = BRI
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.629 option nfa.629.b"
		name = nfa.629.b #Return to France
		trigger = {
			tag = NFA
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = BRI
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #BEL lands back to NFA
	id = nfa.630
	title = nfa.630.t
	desc = nfa.630.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_map_france

	trigger = {
		any_owned_state = { is_european_france = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.630 option nfa.630.a"
		name = nfa.630.a #Send it all away
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_european_france = yes }
				transfer_state_to = NFA
				remove_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = nfa_whole_land days = 10 value = 1 }
			country_event = nfa.631
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.630 option nfa.630.b"
		name = nfa.630.b #Negotiate to keep Dunkirk in exchange for everything else
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_european_france = yes
				NOT = { state = 29 } #Don't give away Dunkirk
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_european_france = yes
					NOT = { state = 29 } #Don't give away Dunkirk
				}
				transfer_state_to = NFA
				remove_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = nfa_some_land days = 10 value = 1 }
			country_event = nfa.631
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.630 option nfa.630.c"
		name = nfa.630.c #Keep the land
		NFA = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = nfa_no_land days = 10 value = 1 }
			country_event = nfa.631
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #BEL offers their response to NFA
	id = nfa.631
	title = nfa.631.t
	desc = {
		text = nfa.631.d1
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nfa_whole_land }
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.631.d2
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nfa_some_land }
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.631.d3
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nfa_no_land }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_map_france

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.631 option nfa.631.a"
		name = nfa.631.a #Thanks for everything
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = nfa_whole_land
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_european_france = yes }
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				remove_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.631 option nfa.631.b"
		name = nfa.631.b #We must settle for the 1918 borders
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = nfa_some_land
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_european_france = yes
					NOT = { state = 29 } #Don't give away Dunkirk
				}
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				remove_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.631 option nfa.631.c"
		name = nfa.631.c #They have kept everything
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = nfa_no_land
		}

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
}

	id = nfa.632
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.632" }
	title = nfa.632.t
	desc = nfa.632.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_OTT_buraimi

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			regional_africa_news = yes
			regional_europe_news = yes
			tag = CAN
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.632.a
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.632.b
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.632.c
		trigger = {
			has_authoritarian_government = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to force the resistance modifier to go back on NFA states that glitch out and don't get the modifier added
	id = nfa.633
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		NFA = {
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = nfa_state_colonial_resistance_flag
						NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance } }
						NOT = { is_core_of = NFA }
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = nfa_state_colonial_exploitation_flag
						NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation } }
						NOT = { is_core_of = NFA }
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event nfa.633 option nfa.633.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Drat
	}
}
